1.1.1 Non-text Content (1 avvik)1 alvorlig
Testregel 1.1.1 (1.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

SVG is missing accessible name

<svg id="logo_stange" viewbox="0 0 301.283 51.143" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
Addelement inside SVG, or aria-label attribute. Use role="presentation" if decorative
1.3.1 Info and Relationships (4 avvik)4 moderat
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

First heading is h2, should start with h1

<h2><span><a href="https://www.stange.kommune.no/naring-miljo-landbruk/" target="_self">Næring, miljø, landbruk</a></span></h2>
Start your heading structure with h1
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Heading level skipped: h1 to h5

<h5 id="newtext-h5-1-26188"><strong>Forslag med begrunnelse kan sendes til <a href="mailto:post@stange.kommune.no ">post@stange.kommune.no </a>innen 4. mai. </strong></h5>
Don't skip heading levels. Use h2 instead of h5
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Heading level skipped: h3 to h6

<h6 id="newtext-h6-1-26188">Tidligere prisvinnere</h6>
Don't skip heading levels. Use h4 instead of h6

Useelement for interactive controls, or add role='button'
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Add text like '(opens in new tab)' or use visually-hidden text for screen readers
